msg:Swan Lake Hotel is the oldest and oldest five-star hotel next to Swan Lake. It has a superior location, convenient transportation, and naturally unmatched scenery.
We booked an executive lake view room. As soon as we entered the room, we were attracted by the scenery outside the window. The large glass window faces the beautiful Swan Lake and the tall buildings on the lakeside, which is very beautiful.
Although I stayed at the Swan Lake Hotel not long after it opened, I didn't choose to stay here again when I came to Hefei because I was worried that the hotel had been open for a long time and the decoration and facilities were old. But this time I was surprised. The room facilities are complete, clean and hygienic, and it doesn't look like an old hotel opened in 2016 at all. It is enough to prove that the hotel management is standardized and the employees are responsible.
Although the degree of intelligence is not as good as that of the newly opened five-star hotels, there are also many highlights here. For example, the self-service check-in management system at the front desk is very fast. There is also the hotel's butler service. After checking in, the butler Renee took the initiative to add WeChat, reply to guests' inquiries at any time, and help solve problems. It is very considerate and very convenient.
The breakfast is quite satisfactory. Compared with the breakfast price of hundreds of yuan in other five-star hotels, this one is very close to the people. The parking lot is large and it is very convenient to park by car. Yintai is next door, which is also very convenient for shopping and eating. The hotel is generally very cost-effective.
